    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

  <span id="freeText11762633488197645664" style="display:none">What if damnation is the price of true love?<br /><br />Innocent blood has been spilled on the steps of the Council Hall, the sacred stronghold of the Shadowhunters. In the wake of the tragic death of Livia Blackthorn, the Clave teeters on the brink of civil war. One fragment of the Blackthorn family flees to Los Angeles, seeking to discover the source of the disease that is destroying the race of warlocks. Meanwhile, Julian and Emma take desperate measures to put their forbidden love aside and undertake a perilous mission to Faerie to retrieve the Black Volume of the Dead. What they find in the Courts is a secret that may tear the Shadow World asunder and open a dark path into a future they could never have imagined. Caught in a race against time, Emma and Julian must save the world of Shadowhunters before the deadly power of the <i>parabatai</i> curse destroys them and everyone they love.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11762633488197645664" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

      </div>
</div>

        $('edition_30214330').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_30214330').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });

      $('span_class_gr-hyperlink_sort_order_span_tip_153').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>    </div>
</div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2425149252" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16163305550707222088"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544559136i/26730454._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Bones</a> ★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Ashes</a> ★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Glass</a> ★★★<br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br/>4.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br/>5.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br/>3.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br/>6.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362' rel='nofollow noopener'>The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842' rel='nofollow noopener'>Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a> ★★★<br/>1.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570227019' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lady Midnight</a> ★★★★★<br/>2.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2589314651' rel='nofollow noopener'>Lord of Shadows</a> ★★★★<br/>*.) <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2598539473' rel='nofollow noopener'>Ghosts of the Shadow Market</a> 8/10<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There was blood on the Council dais, blood on the steps, blood on the walls and the floor and the shattered remnant</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText16163305550707222088" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544559136i/26730454._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> ★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2373838717" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Ashes</a> ★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2463489480" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Glass</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2465856942" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a> ★★★<br>4.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2489169365" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Fallen Angels</a> ★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2518308849" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a> ★★★★<br>5.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2526157370" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Lost Souls</a> ★★★★<br>3.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2531117647" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a> ★★★★★<br>6.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2544728646" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a> ★★★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2552335362" rel="nofollow noopener">The Bane Chronicles</a> ★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2564114842" rel="nofollow noopener">Tales from the Shadowhunter Academy</a> ★★★<br>1.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2570227019" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a> ★★★★★<br>2.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2589314651" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Shadows</a> ★★★★<br>*.) <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2598539473" rel="nofollow noopener">Ghosts of the Shadow Market</a> 8/10<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There was blood on the Council dais, blood on the steps, blood on the walls and the floor and the shattered remnants of the Mortal Sword.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Friends, it has been a ride. I have spent the last six months reading everything that Cassie Clare has created for the Shadowhunter world, and it was all leading up to this moment – the release of <i>Queen of Air and Darkness</i>. And friends, it was so worth it. Not only was reading all of these books and stories, and falling in love with so many of these characters and worlds, a highlight in my reading year, it was just a highlight in my 2018. And I just want to thank each and every single one of you that came along with me on this journey. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Blood always matters, to the wrong sort of people”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And this book picks up immediately after the events in <i>LoS</i>. Fascists are trying to control the Clave and dictate how Downworlders should be treated. In Faerie, the Seelie and the Unseelie court are trying to hurt each other, while the Unseelie King has something that the Seelie Queen doesn’t want to live without. Warlocks are hurting, so many of our main cast of characters are missing, and so many people are grieving the loss of loved ones. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Sympathy is common. Knowing the exact shape of the hole someone’s loss leaves in your heart is rare.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>Queen of Air and Darkness</i> is truly a love letter to grief. The first section of this review is going to be spoiler free, so I’m going to try to be really vague. Ty is choosing to ignore his grief, Alec is throwing himself into work and wanting a better world because of his grief, Julian thinks revenge is the only way to work through his grief, Emma has finally made headway with her past grief, to only be forced to experience more all over again. We see parents grieving the loss of their children, children grieving the loss of their parents, and everyone grieving the loss of loved ones because of wars they didn’t ask to be a part of. But that’s what happens when you love people, and you let them in, because nothing is permanent, and grief is inevitable. There is no wrong way to grieve, but you do get to choose the actions you perform in the name of that grief. And we get to see people make a lot of hateful choices, and take a lot of hateful actions, because of their grief; Cohorts and fae queens and kings alike.<br><br>And this third and final installment in <i>The Dark Artifices</i> series does get rather dark, so please use caution. <b>Content and trigger warnings</b> for hate speech (always challenged and always negative), threatening to out someone, talk of wanting to sexually assault someone, self-harm, death, loss of a loved one, murder, torture, captivity, blood depictions, strong depictions of grief, trauma, and depression, talk of suicide, a lot of violence, and war themes. <br><br>As always, Cassie is so very inclusionary and gives us so much rep that is very respectively done. From so much sexuality and gender representation, to racial diversity, to giving us a main character on the autism spectrum, to body diversity, to really respecting mental health in this book. I’m not saying that Cassie Clare is the pinnacle of what representation in books should be, but I’ll be dammed if she isn’t trying, and if she isn’t doing a better job than any other cis white woman writing YA currently. <br><br>Overall, it is also actually wild how talented Cassandra Clare is, because the cast of her books are so large and expansive, but I’d die for almost every single one of them. I had so much fun reading this last installment, even if it wasn’t my favorite. But I will talk more about that below! I will say that I need <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2612221563" rel="nofollow noopener">The Red Scrolls of Magic</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2603395082" rel="nofollow noopener">The Last Hours</a>, &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2613165573" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wicked Powers</a> right this very second. Like, the wait is probably going to kill me. But I’m going to die with the biggest smile on my face. <br><br><b>Please use caution reading the rest of this review if you have not read this book and all the series leading up to this book!</b> And as always, I’m going to do a little mini character breakdown on my thoughts and feelings on all the main characters in this book. <b>Spoilers ahead!</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1544252151i/26712737._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Art by <a href="https://twitter.com/aliceduke/status/1045707679627382789" rel="nofollow noopener">Alice Duke</a>!)<br><br>➽ <b>Emma Carstairs</b> - You all, I can’t even talk about Emma properly. She is my favorite Shadowhunter of them all. I love her, I love her bravery, I love her empathy, and I love how she loves. I’ll be honest, the worst part about turning the last page of this book is knowing that I’ll never be able to read another new book where she is the main character. <br><br>➽ <b>Julian Blackthorn</b> - First off, <a href="https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=n1grAMSMwm8" rel="nofollow noopener">Madalyn</a> pointing out that Julian is probably demisexual added ten years to my life and I needed you all to know this. Next, Julian Blackthorn is my everything and I hate that I’m so weak for this soft boy, but it is the damn truth. <br><br>Also, because I’m a perv and this needs to be said, Julian and Emma reciting the parabatai vow while fucking? My kink. My fucking kink. Damn. The gifts CC gives us. <br><br>➽ <b>Church</b> - The real MVP of this book. <br><br>➽ <b>Helen Blackthorn-Penhallow</b> - Helen and Aline are going to be the best moms ever, and I am so happy that Cassie finally let us see this power couple! And I can’t wait to actually see them fall in love during TRSoM, but I know it is going to be my favorite thing in this entire series! <br><br>➽ <b>Aline Blackthorn-Penhallow</b> - Okay, Helen and Aline are my TRUE OTP! And Aline literally give me life, while standing up for Helen, during this entire 900+ page story. And I’m here for any story that is a bout an Asian girl getting into a sapphic relationship with a fae girl. I mean, it is kind of my life goal. <br><br>➽ <b>Mark Blackthorn</b> - You all, we did it, and CC answered our prayers! And she gave us the polyamorous relationship of my dreams! I will say that I don’t entirely love that they only have their cabin to share their love, but I hope that a lot happens in future books to make this trio able to truly spend all of their lives with one another. But that scene on the boulder between the three of them? 11/10, I will be rereading once a week for the rest of my life. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“All this time we were waiting for you. We loved each other, and it was a great thing, but with you, it is even greater.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Cristina Rosales</b> - I just love Cristina. I love her friendship with Emma, but I loved her deciding, at her own pace, what she wanted in her life. And she’s so damn strong, while being so damn giving, and she honestly deserves the entire world. Also, no offense, but Cassie Clare also gave her the worst Shadowhunter weapons, imo. <br><br>➽ <b>Kieran</b> - I mean, you all know I’m trash for dark (ever changing) haired fae princes who end up being king. But like, I’d love Kieran even if he was none of those things. He is honestly probably my third favorite character in all of the Shadowhunter world. And when all the fae people were remembering all the kind things he did for them, and when the little girl gave him the white flower? Friends, I’m weak, and soft, and crying, and in love with Kieran so very much. <br><br>➽ <b>Adaon</b> - Wow, the resident sleeper and true hero of this story. <br><br>➽ <b>Kit Rook / Christopher Herondale</b> - Alright, Kit is going to have the coolest power(s) in the Shadowhunter world. But I truly loved how this book officially proved that Kit is going to have an actual claim to rule all of Faerie, and I’m here for it. <br><br>➽ <b>Tiberius Blackthorn</b> - Oh Ty, my sweet Ty. You know this necromancy and dark magic are going to follow him all the way through TWP! You all also know that I’m a sucker for siblings who are best friends, and Thule Livvy’s letter actually gutted me. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I love you. I love you. I love you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Livvy Blackthorn</b> - I don’t really understand how ghost Livvy works, or how the connection with Ty works, but it equally breaks and warms my heart. But I do really wish she would have just been able to rest in peace.<br><br>➽ <b>Octavian Blackthorn</b> - I feel like Poor Tavvy is the character that is looked over, but it is because he is still so little. But I cried really hard when he told Julian that he just wanted to go home at the end. Julian really raised all these kids to be brave, to be strong, and to love always. <br><br>➽ <b>Dru Blackthorn</b> - Dru truly has grown up and came into her own during these three books. I love her, and I loved seeing her journey. And I especially loved seeing Ty spend more time with her. I can’t wait to see her grow and shine even more in TWP where she will be a main character. <br><br>➽ <b>Ash</b> - Did Cassie really have to give him Rhysand wings? Truly? Honestly? Lord, why? But… I’m here for it, and I also ship him and Drusilla so damn hard already. When he picked up that picture that Julian drew and learned her name? I screamed. I can’t wait for that to make another appearance. <br><br>➽ <b>Magnus Bane</b> - You all know Magnus is my favorite. Every book I fall more and more in love with him. And seeing him as a dad? It is truly the best. Also, Magnus having a heart to heart with Ty about gutted me, because it was so damn beautiful. <br><br>➽ <b>Alec Lightwood</b> - I honestly feel like Alec was a real shining star in this book. And he is going to completely change the world with unconditional love. And seeing him become Consul of the Clave? I don’t even have words. Alec started out as a character that was hard for me to like, now he’s a character that’s hard for me not to love. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“No shining new world could be built on blood and bones.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>➽ <b>Zara Dearborn</b> - Worst part of this book? That Zara didn’t die. And now she has her own little private city to breed her hate. I am so not looking forward to what is going to come of her and her hateful gang being left alone. Real talk, I would have been like, “We will leave all you Cohorts alone, as long as you give us her!” <i>*winky face*</i> I’m a petty and bitter bitch. <br><br>➽ <b>Horace Dearborn</b> - Thank you, next. <br><br>➽ <b>The Kelpie (that Julian saved)</b> - I always love the magical creatures of stories, that come and help and save that day. But this was too damn much for me. TOO DAMN MUCH. <br><br>➽ <b>Manuel Casales</b> - This guy is so chaotic evil. And I’m so bitter that he didn’t die while Emma and Julian were on their wild rampage. <br><br>➽ <b>Diego Rosales</b> - I also really couldn’t ever truly like Diego. Yeah, he did Kieran a solid, and I respect it, but I still never really liked him. He is one of the few side characters I’m okay saying goodbye to. <br><br>➽ <b>Jaime Rosales</b> - I feel like CC is just going to give Dru all the options between Ash, Cameron, and Jaime, but Jaime is the one that skeezes me out for some reason. I just, don’t want it to happen. Nice dagger gift and all, boy no. <br><br>➽ <b>Diana Wrayburn</b> - I will say that I was a little uncomfortable with how Julian and Emma found out about Diana being trans, but I am honestly just so happy that she is living her best life now, while being able to be open. And the talk she has with Julian and Emma, when she is like, “No, I’ve always been a woman.” Praise/bless. Give me an entire Diana series, please, Cassie Clare. <br><br>➽ <b>Gwyn</b> - Wow, the best character in the entire Shadowhunter universe. The blessings. <br><br>➽ <b>Catarina Loss</b> - Catarina is the best side character, and she does so much good, and she is so pure, and I wept extra hard when she stood by Magnus at his wedding. Like, these warlocks put me in my feels every single time. <br><br>➽ <b>Ragnor Fell / Shade</b> - And this warlock just makes me laugh so damn hard. And I cheered out loud when the reveal actually came to fruition! I can’t wait to see even more of him with Ty in Scholomance. <br><br>➽ <b>Annabel Blackthorn</b> - What a missed opportunity in this book to not give Annabel a better story. I’ll talk more about this below, but Annabel deserved better, especially with how breathtaking this cover it.<br><br>➽ <b>The (old) Unseelie King</b> - I don’t know if I just forgot, or if I never picked up on it, but this dude had a half skeletal, half handsome face? That’s actually badass. <br><br>➽ <b>The Seelie Queen</b> - This bitch. She legit just shows up in every book, in every timeline, just to rain on everyone’s parade. <br><br>➽ <b>Tessa &amp; Jem</b> - I screamed all over again after they announced they were pregnant. And now that they are going to raise a Herondale, Kit, so he can be safe? Ah, I just love this little family so much.<br><br>➽ <b>Izzy &amp; Simon</b> - I really wish they played bigger roles in this story, and that we would have received two weddings in this 900+ page tome!<br><br>➽ <b>Clary Fairchild</b> - I won’t lie, I was really disappointed when we found out what Clary’s vision really was. God, I mean, I knew Cassie wouldn’t actually kill her, but I wanted to so much more, and it was a really anticlimactic reasoning. <br><br>➽ <b>Jace Herondale</b> - <i>“I would die for Jace to shoot finger guns at me”</i> - <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/drumsofautumn" rel="nofollow noopener">Lea</a>, 2018. Real talk, Jace had me actually laughing out loud during this entire book and I loved and hated every single second of it. Especially his banter with Kit, I mean, Christopher. And when Jace voted in Alec for Consul of the Clave? The tears just won’t stop, friends. <br><br>➽ <b>Evil Jace Herondale</b> - Lord, why do you want us to suffer? <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“There is nothing simple about vengeance, and nothing pure”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Okay, so one element or “trope” that I hate when books do is that alternate and/or parallel universe storyline. And I never, in a million years, would have guessed that Cassie Clare would pull this in <i>QoAaD</i>, but here we are. I’ll be honest, I kind of loved the concept of a <i>Mad Max</i> world where Sebastian Morgenstern not only won the Dark War, but now rules, but the entirety of Part Two was a little too much for me. Especially because they didn’t even bring back Thule Livvy and Thule Raphael. And in return, it almost felt like tragedy porn seeing them live again. And now we have an evil Jace in our world and on the loose to… kill Clary? Love Clary? To do something with Clary? Yikes. <br><br>But the true reason I am giving this book four stars, and the reason I probably think it is the weakest book in <i>The Dark Artifices</i> is because of Annabel. What a missed opportunity to have an amazing villain character. Instead, she dies at 60%, only for us to be rickrolled with a demon pretending to be her. She died so easily, too, and it felt so bad. I mean, she is on the cover of this book! And the title is completely her! Why would she barely show up in the 900+ pages, have the lamest death, and have no character development when she could have been such an amazing and intricate character. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Please don’t leave me in this world without you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>And then let’s not forget about Julian and Emma turning into giant, angel versions of <i>King Kong</i>, picking up and yeeting the bad guys. Even though, Zara conveniently didn’t get yeeted. Like, for a second I actually thought Emma was going to die, and then, in turn, Julian would have died, too. But when Emma said, <i>“Let us burn.”</i> I thought they would just die and become angels together, and my emo and sappy ass would have loved that. But instead, the whole wild giant thing happened, and then words of their loved ones “healed” them. Which was eyeroll worthy, but also sweet. Yet, when the heavenly fire didn’t damage ANYTHING except their parabatai bond? You all, I can’t. It just feels so unsatisfying. And Emma and Julian really are my favorite couple in all things Shadowhunter, but even I can’t just accept that and pretend it was realistic. I honestly think CC just wrote herself into a hole, and putting a bright and shiny bow on it was the only option, but it doesn’t mean I have to like it. <br><br>I will also say that the ending was completely and utterly fanservice, but it was fanservice that I ate up with a spoon and asked for more. Magnus and Alec’s wedding was everything, and Alec’s proposal made me actually ugly cry. Just seeing everything that these two have been through, all the lives they’ve impacted, all the family they have made, they were just so damn deserving of this happiness. And then the short story after the epilogue? With Jace and Clary in that greenhouse? God, that greenhouse. It really feels so full circle, doesn’t it? All of these original characters have brought me so much happiness in 2018, and seeing them get moments of pure happiness at the end of this book was honestly everything. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“As long as you exist and I exist, I will love you.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Overall, I’d give my life for Emma Carstairs and any of the Blackthorns and I will never forget this reading experience. Picking up <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2008644944" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> this year was one of the best decisions I’ve ever made. And now I finally get to wait and suffer for the next thing Cassie Clare publishes with the rest of you! And special thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2205066030" rel="nofollow noopener">Lea</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2454987139" rel="nofollow noopener">Sol</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2081510149" rel="nofollow noopener">Madalyn</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2615201108" rel="nofollow noopener">Jane</a>, &amp; <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1583649783" rel="nofollow noopener">Amber</a> for allowing me to cry and scream and gush with you! You all made the experience even more special and I love you all! ❤<br><br><a href="https://meltotheany.wordpress.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/meltotheany/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.twitter.com/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://meltotheany.tumblr.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a> | <a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UC4RbHEg_fH6CewJrh_0xJ9g" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> | <a href="http://www.twitch.tv/meltotheany" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitch</a> </span>

  <div class="friendReviews elementListBrown" >
    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_2575341745" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745" />
    <a title="Elle (ellexamines)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/52545435-elle-ellexamines"><img alt="Elle (ellexamines)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1582250895p2/52545435.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2575341745?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle (ellexamines)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle (ellexamines)" href="/user/show/52545435-elle-ellexamines">Elle (ellexamines)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=x-series">x-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=sff-pn-urban-fantasy">sff-pn-urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=y-out2018">y-out2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=3-star">3-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/52545435-elle-ellexamines?shelf=z-read2019">z-read2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2575341745" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2160560179931587027">This was... a whole mess.<br/>**Spoilers are marked in text, and in case character talk was what you were here for, <b>I keysmashed a bit at the bottom of this page.</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽P A C I N G I S S U E S G A L O R E </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Fuck, you guys, the scope and pacing of this was <i>wild ride</i>. <b>Generally, this just felt very thrown together in comparison to the fairly well-balanced nature of earlier books.</b> <br/><br/>Let’s talk some details.<br/><br/>First of all, the <i>concept</i> of Thule… is good. [And <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2425149252?book_show_action=false' rel='nofollow noopener'>Melanie’s description of it</a> as a <i>Mad Max</i> versi</span>
  <span id="freeText2160560179931587027" style="display:none">This was... a whole mess.<br>**Spoilers are marked in text, and in case character talk was what you were here for, <b>I keysmashed a bit at the bottom of this page.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽P A C I N G I S S U E S G A L O R E </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Fuck, you guys, the scope and pacing of this was <i>wild ride</i>. <b>Generally, this just felt very thrown together in comparison to the fairly well-balanced nature of earlier books.</b> <br><br>Let’s talk some details.<br><br>First of all, the <i>concept</i> of Thule… is good. [And <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2425149252?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Melanie’s description of it</a> as a <i>Mad Max</i> version of the Shadowhunters world is honestly real.] BUT it takes up about a quarter of this 900 (nine hundred) page book, and it. has. no. bearing. on the plot. until the <i>epilogue</i>. in which it is used to <b>set up <i>another whole ass trilogy</i></b>.<br><br>Also, what the <i>fuck</i> happened with Annabelle? Annabelle honestly has one of the better villain setups Cassie has ever pulled off, and the fact that she does nothing except die, and dies halfway through the book is just. It’s just a mess. I hate it. <br><br>Just as in… every one of CC’s conclusions I’ve read, I think the first five chapters or so should have been incorporated into the last book. She has a tendency to set up The Final Showdown conflicts at the beginning of the third book rather than at the end of the second, which messes with her flow, leaving us with abrupt book two endings (Lord of Shadows. i loved that book but admit it, this is a problem) and <b>lacking buildup for events in book three.</b><br><br>Here is a simple way this couldve been done to this particular book: end it not on the note of <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Livia’s death <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>, but on the note of Julian’s trip to see Magnus. This both makes the ending of book two less abrupt and, more importantly, given how weirdly disconnected some of this conflict feels, sets up an approximate book three conflict. <br><br>Oh, and speaking of villains, remember how Zara was going to die and I was going to be all<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1540681565ra/26510246.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yeah. I don’t either. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽F A N S E R V I C E I N P S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Remember back in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">my review of book one</a>, when Jace and Clary’s heavyhanded but brief cameo was the most I’ve liked them in the entire canon of the universe, and yes it was fanservice but it was <i>fun</i>? Oh man. Good old days. This could have been <i>The Mortal Instruments book #7, City of I Don’t Give A Shit</i> for all the TMI presence. <br><br>I don’t even know if I’m referring to stuff with earlier characters, because I actually don’t mind that too much. Magnus and Alec, two of the only characters in TMI I actually like, have stopped being done dirty finally; Jem and Tessa are two of my favorite fictional characters and I can’t even pretend to complain about their cameo; even though I never got to their minor presence in TMI part two, Helen and Aline are amazing. <b>So maybe it’s not even about the fanservice; it’s just that the. scope. is. so. so. wide.</b> By this, I am of course referring to: Thule, and the return of Sebastian Morgenstern and his secret?? son?? a character I will not even pretend to give a shit about. And also Emo Jace. <br><br>And okay, listen, I know Cassandra Clare isn’t exactly trying to get all of her work done completely sans-fanservice: the investment in the characters and relationships is the backbone of her work, what makes it so easy to enjoy. But unlike some of her other books, this just… fell flat? It feels like the heart, the enthusiasm, <b>the genuine love</b> that she poured into <i>The Infernal Devices</i> and earlier books in this series was just... <b>missing.</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽T H E A C T U A L E N D I N G</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Uh, so first of all, I will say that I didn’t totally 100% hate the actual ending. I just didn't really feel it was built up enough. And to me, it demonstrated just how little progress was made within this book.<br><br>Here's the thing: of the three main character dynamics used for conflict within this series — Christina &amp; Kieran &amp; Mark, Kit &amp; Ty, and Julian &amp; Emma — <b>only one is genuinely resolved.</b> And the thing is, this lack of resolution sort of works; one dynamic is about half-resolved and just dealing with problems, and one is not even <i>close</i> to being resolved but they're getting a whole series written about them, so fine. But I think my overwhelming feeling upon first finishing this book was... wow, is that all we're resolving? Is that all the progress we've made? Really, in 900 pages? In that case... couldn't it have just been 500 pages?<br><br>Moving on. The final battle is... sort of cool, but it is awkwardly written, and feels fairly contrived. We know <i>something</i> magic is going to happen at the end, and we hope it'll lead to a somewhat decent ending, but the buildup falls apart just a little on the way. On that topic: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[no one dying. See, I actually hate major character death, so I can’t really pretend to be upset about this, but no one really gets <i>changed permanently</i> by the battle, either. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> To me, it just feels like this series has been pretending the ending is going to make us all sooooo sad, and it doesn't. It's a series about hope and coming together, which is great — it just shouldn't be talked about as a tragic romance, that's all. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽I S W E A R, I D I D N’ T H A T E I T</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Um… I thought the first 20% or so of this book was really pretty solid? This section was also a lot funnier! Examples of this phenomenon include: <br>➽“and- julian is like sebastian morgenstern!” *cue Diego laughing really hard*<br>Julian putting his boots on Horace’s desk like a legend<br>➽“you two have really fucked up.” <br>➽“ever wanted to move objects with your mind?” “sure, sounds great!” <br>➽“who hates you? I’ll kill them!” which is just a deeply Aline thing to say<br><br>I’ve sort of alluded to this already, but the most coherent main theme of this book is the idea of grieving for the lost being a necessary process, and when that theme stands out amongst the generally muddled plot, it’s handled well. Julian’s arc around grief is nuanced and fairly well-handled; Emma’s arc has sort of always been about grief, it’s just that this book realizes it better than earlier books. Ty’s arc around grief is honestly just kind of heartbreaking. Kieran’s arc focuses more around finding forgiveness, but it feels coherent with the rest of the arcs. Alec’s arc (I know) is around worrying about eventual grief and is… honestly better than any character arc he got in TMI? SORRY. <br><br>For those of you in the comments saying I’m rating generously… I mean, I guess I am. But I can’t actually give this book two stars because, as I deepdived into in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">previous</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">reviews</a> (#shamelessselfpromo), <b>I like these characters way too much.</b> <br><br>OH AND. You all know I’ve been talking about this nonstop, but Mark and Christina and Kieran!! Being a canon dynamic!! I really really wanted more out of their buildup, to be honest, because it’s been utterly fantastic up to this book and felt sort of meh here, but <b>I’m just. So so happy. That the polyamorous trio is canon.</b> I’ve been waiting six months but the rest of you have all been waiting years so round of applause for that!!<br><br>I also think, removing all critique, that juggling ten to fifteen lead characters with any degree of success is <i>incredibly</i> difficult, and the fact that this is even somewhat pulled off is really impressive. I mean, even putting important-in-the-future characters like Dru (who deserved more airtime), Tavvy, Dark Livvy, Gwyn (the only man i trust), Cameron, Jaime (who i dislike. just facts), Diego (who i now love!!), and Ash (??) to the side, and even eliminating villains like Zara, Manuel, Horace, the Seelie Queen, the Unseelie King, Annabel, Sebastian, and Dark Jace, and even <i>not</i> counting the massive presence of TMI characters like Helen, Aline, Jace, Clary, Magnus, Alec, and Ragnor Fel — several of whom <i>have actual character arcs in this book</i> — we <i>still</i> have Julian and Emma, Mark and Christina and Kieran, Kit and Ty, and Diana starring as genuine leading characters. <b>That’s a total of thirty-one names including eight leads.</b> Impressive as fuck. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>➽E N D I N G T H O U G H T S</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>No one has ever accused me of being coherent. <br>→this series could also be called Julian Makes A Bad Decision: News at 11<br>→Everything Diana And Gwyn Have Ever Done. It’s Flawless And Good<br>→There was a line in this book in which Aline’s posture is described as “straight,” which is something no self-respecting gay would write without making a joke. That’s not a flaw. I just think I’m funnier than I actually am.<br><br>Anyway. Yes, as we’ve discussed, the entire existence of this whole world is kind of ridiculous, but I’m not going to pretend I don’t kind of love it. I just wish this conclusion had come through a bit more.<br><br><b>
  <i>looking out for:</i>
</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2483323177" rel="nofollow noopener">The Red Scrolls of Magic</a> | 2 April 2019<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2625780720" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a> | 19 November 2019<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2654466524" rel="nofollow noopener">The Wicked Powers</a> | sometime, 2022<br><br><b>
  <i>dark artifices reviews:</i>
</b> <br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2435531671" rel="nofollow noopener">book one</a> | ★★★★★<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2569455643" rel="nofollow noopener">book two</a> | ★★★★★<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2575341745" rel="nofollow noopener">book three</a> | ★★★☆☆<br><br><a href="https://thebookishactress.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/thebookishactress" rel="nofollow noopener">Goodreads</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/jespergayhey" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/thebookishactress/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://www.youtube.com/c/thebookishactress" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781471116704" href="/book/show/30214330-queen-of-air-and-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=f-f">f-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=favourite-covers">favourite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=gay-mc">gay-mc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=lgbtqiap">lgbtqiap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=owned-books">owned-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fave-couple">fave-couple</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7706640-jamieson?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1584091974" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13906136269146384204">this truly WAS the infinity war of the shadowhunter chronicles, it was so wild to see so many characters from across this universe play a role here and I LOVED IT.<br/><br/><br/> <b>I've had like a month to process this book and okay</b> like I don't think my brain and heart will EVER be able to process what this book just did to me but I'm going to try. So, yes below you can read my <b>
  <u>FULL REVIEW OF QUEEN OF AIR AND DARKNESS</u>
</b><br/><br/> (also, I'm saying now I CANNOT PROMISE THIS REVIEW WILL BE SPOILER FREE OK YOU WERE WARNED</span>
  <span id="freeText13906136269146384204" style="display:none">this truly WAS the infinity war of the shadowhunter chronicles, it was so wild to see so many characters from across this universe play a role here and I LOVED IT.<br /><br /><br /> <b>I've had like a month to process this book and okay</b> like I don't think my brain and heart will EVER be able to process what this book just did to me but I'm going to try. So, yes below you can read my <b>
  <u>FULL REVIEW OF QUEEN OF AIR AND DARKNESS</u>
</b><br /><br /> (also, I'm saying now I CANNOT PROMISE THIS REVIEW WILL BE SPOILER FREE OK YOU WERE WARNED)<br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“The sky was a road and the stars made pathways; the moon was a watchtower, a lighthouse that led you home.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br />This book was <u>easily</u> my most anticipated book of the year. I had made a big claim that if Queen lived up to Clockwork Princess, then The Dark Artifices would become my new favourite series of Cassandra Clare's. I don't know how I feel about that now. This ending wasn't as good as the Clockwork Princess ending for me, but there was SO many things I loved about it. I loved the characters, (most) of the plot, the angst, the romance, and seeing all the different series come together (most of the time). But there was some things (the lst 100 pages) that annoyed me so I just couldn't give it a five star even though it SHOULD HAVE BEEN ..... it COULD HAVE BEEN ....... im furious ! Anyways, lets break this bad bitch down: <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“I whisper your name, Ty. I whisper the most important thing: <br />I love you. I love you. I love you.<br />Livvy” <br /><br /></blockquote>
</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>CHARACTERS</u>
</b><br /><br /><b>Lets start with characters because it's my favourite part of this series</b><br /><br /><b>Emma</b> remains my favourite character, what an iconic queen. I honestly ADORE Emma and she's one of my favourite CC characters ever. She's changed and developed so much between book one and three, but I love what a strong badass she is whilst also being caring and compassionate and maintaining important relationships. It's nice to have a female character who'd badass and blunt but not necessarily <i>cold</i>. I literally love her, and I really want her to punch me in the face because it'd be an HONOUR. <br /><br /><b>Julian</b> for some reason a lot of people don't like Julian but I LOVE JULIAN. He's such an interesting and unusual main male character, especially from Cassandra Clare. So I think he adds a really great dimension to this series and is such a contrast to characters like Will or Jace. AND ANTI-HERO JULIAN FINALLY KINDA ROSE AND I WAS SCARED. All in all I loved his arc in this book .. the dark julian contrasted with actual julian was painful to read but I loved it. YOU ARE IN THE CAGE? I cried. Also, I just love Dad! Julian and how he treats his entire family dfjghdfkj.<b> ALSO WE LOVE A DEMISEXUAL !! KING!!!!!</b><br /><br /><b>Mark, Cristina and Kieran</b> SO I have always felt meh about Mark. I don't dislike him .. I actually like him quite a bit. I just don't like him as much as some people seem to. I felt pretty much the same about him in this as I always have. I love Cristina and I loved her in this too. But I felt she didn't get as good an arc as the other characters? Her entire plot was pretty much romance which was kind of annoying though I DID LOVE HER TEAM UP IN FAERIE. ICONIC!! Kieran I still feel mixed on. I've never liked him much but he did grow on me a bit in this. I actually kinda ended up liking him even though I still don't care about him on the same level as the other characters. But his character arc was great. <br /><br /><b>Kit and Ty</b> THEY WERE NOT IN THIS ENOUGH?? Okay yes they literally had a major plot arc BUT STILL. Ty should of have a POV but he never did! I also hated the conclusion of their arc ... obviously it's going to be the main focus of The Wicked Powers but it was SO unsatisfying here. I also though Ty's literally had no growth in the 700 pages of this book which was annoying. But I LOVED KIT SO MUCH. Thats my son !!!! I really liked his role in this book and his POVs were some of my favourite. He is fucking iconic and hilarious .. "you are so forked", bitch you better BET i laughed<br /><br /><b>Dru</b> My unexpected fave of this book. In Lord of Shadows I liked Dru but felt I didn't really know her. She had SO much development and growth in this and I loved her role. I didn't expect to love her so much but I seriously do, and I think of all the characters I am MOST excited to see more of DRU in The Wicked Powers! She stole my heart, I love her. <br /><br /><b>Jaimie and Diego</b> They were in this more than I expected and I didn't .. love it. Honestly I did Not like Diego's chapters much, I just don't care about them that much so their chapters were always the ones that made me want to put this book down. But I did like their characters in relation to their character arc with Cristina.<br /><br /><b>Diana </b> I LOVE DIANA and I honestly don't have heaps more to say about her?? I liked how she became a more important role in the Clave in this book and I also liked how there was more focus on her being an older sister to Emma and Julian in this. <br /><br /><b>Helen and Aline </b> MY SAPPHIC QUEEEENS ! I love both of them so much. Aline was such a fun character because she was so different to Helen and even to Jules and Emma in terms of how she handled the kids. Helen was sweet and I LOVED her relationship with Mark in this. Seeing those two interact were some of my favourite parts of this book. Aline and Helen are also so fucking cute jghfkgj it's unfair of Ms Clare to show us gays a pair of gfs that cute when she KNOWS none of us can achieve that irl because all gays are too useless to actually date other gays. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“Grief can be so bad you can’t breathe, but that’s what it means to be human. We lose, we suffer, but we have to keep breathing.” </blockquote>
</i><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <u>PLOT</u>
</b><br /><br />Queen of Air and Darkness picks up right where Lord of Shadows ends. I loved this choice but also I WAS IN SO MUCH PAIN. The scenes of Julian crying and Ty passing out were hard to read and seriously I was emotionally wrecked by page 25 I literally had to take a break. <br /><br />I pretty thoroughly enjoyed the first third of this book. The chapters in faerie were exciting and I liked seeing so many different characters play a role. Simon, Isabelle, Jace, Clary and more appearing was so fun and I loved the cameos. The plot in faerie reminded me a lot of Lord of Shadows but I decided I didn't mind it. That fight in the throne room also reminded me of that fight scene in The Last Jedi with Kylo/Rey and bitch I was HOLLERING. <br /><br />The only plot in the first third I wasn't a fan of was Julian's emotions things - I didn't think it was bad but it just came out of nowhere? In no previous books, even when Emma and Julian discuss their "options" did him removing his emotions come up so it felt out of nowhere and kind of lazy? <br /><br />The second part in Thule was literally my favourite part of the book which seems to be an unpopular opinion, but I thought it was SO MUCH FUN. It was like a canon AU and I was loving it. Seeing the world as it would have been was interesting, and I loved Emma and Julian's arc in this. The focus on their romance and Julian's choices was great and Thule really allowed a lot of emotional catharsis and tangible contrast between what is and what could have been. ALSO JULIAN AND EMMA FUCKING WHILST SAYING THEIR PARABATAI VOWS WAS HOT AND LITERALLY IS MY KINK<br /><br />The final section was my least favourite and where everything seemed to fall apart. <b>I felt Cassandra Clare had so many thread and plots and character things to work with and they ended up not coming together great</b>. It definitely felt like she lost control of the story a bit. The climax was .. incredibly disappointing and so cliche. Again, the whole "Nephilim Parabatai" thing just came literally out of nowhere. The ending of Julian and Emma's complications with being Parabatai was so lazy and wasn't even foreshadowed as a legitimate option until it randomly happened. Using heavenly fire again also felt lazy and the whole "family talks you down" thing was SO cliche. I felt so unsatisfied with the ending here, and I really just can't get over Emma and Julian randomly going giant, throwing around the evil elf army like what the FUCK even was that. It was just messy and weird. <br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“Be good, my archer boy. Come back to me.” <br /><br /></blockquote>
</i><br /><b>
  <u>ROMANCE &amp; ANGST</u>
</b><br /><br />So where the plot let me down, the angst came THROUGH. Honestly I was going into this wanting some sweet, sweet, painful angst and phew, once again the good sis Cassandra delivered. <br /><br />JULIAN AND EMMA .... *kisses fingers* oh yeah thats the STUFF. Like I've said multiple times, I adore them. ADORE THEM. I honestly love their friendship/relationship so much and the whole set up of them being best friend, literally Being Eachother's People, like no one loves them as much as they love eachother ... oh fuck YES thats the shit. I THRIVE off of that. And she delivered in spades .. she really did. AND OH THE ANGST OF DARK! JULIAN. And Dark! Julian being like lowkey hot ... yeah I'm into that. Anyway, truly excellence once again. <br /><br />Mark, Cristina and Kieran ... FINALLY the OT3 we all love and deserve. I see you boring bitches whining about the ending of this love triangle but it is WHAT. WE. DESERVE. Turning your love triangle into a polyam ship? inspired. And it honestly was so well written? That they're all equally in love with eachother?? That Mark/Cristina or Mark/Kieran or Kieran/Cristina doesnt even work because they're all thinking about one another like .. it's mess and I adore it? And the three way ship is perfect?? BUT THE ENDIGN .... I hate that omg ! It was so unresolved which was annoying as fuck but also I stan King Kieran so idk phew that is a tough one. I feel it will also be resolved in The Wicked Powers (IM HOPING)<br /><br />Ty and Kit ... they're so cute aw man. I love Kit's inner monologue around Ty, he's so enamoured with him in such a pure and cute way and there is definitely going to be an arc around him Realising He Is Queer which should be fun. He really is the bi king I deserved. And Ty always recruiting Kit and trusting Kit was so sweet, they're both sweet and even tho I'm an angst DEMON I was rooting for them and their softness. <br /><br />Jace and Clary. LOOK ALL I AM GOING TO SAY IS THEM GOING BACK TO THE GREENHOUSE TO WHERE IT ALL STARTED HAD ME EMO AND ALSO THEM BOTH BUYING A RING ....... INSPIRED<br /><br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“You might be in the cage, Jules, but as long as you are like this, I am in the cage with you.”</blockquote>
</i><br /><br /><b>
  <u>ISSUES</u>
</b><br /><br />Alright the gush has been real now it's time to do some quick rants x <br /><br />Although I loved the Thule chapters, I had one huge issue and that is MAKING SEBASTIAN THE VILLAIN. Sebastian is the one behind all this nonsense and I HATE THAT. It is SO lazy to just bring an old dead villain back, and it's fucking annoying. What is the point of TMI and killing Sebastian if random alternate universe Sebastian can just return to fuck it up? I thought that was so lazy, and completely the opposite of what I had come to expect from CC in this trilogy. In Lady Midnight, Malcolm being the villain completely subverted my expectations because she kept setting up warlock = good, and then she undermined it, which was neat. Malcolm was also such a strong villain with interesting and complex motivations. And while I love Sebastian as a villain, he doesn't fit here, and he's just pure evil, which is fun in tmi but ultimately boring to repeat over and over. I felt CC really let down the great start to the series and intricate plot she had set up. <br /><br />I also was ... so sick of the cameos. Does anyone else wish she would just let TMI go?? At first they were fun, but they started to totally eclipse the other, main characters. I don't want a continuation of their plots, I want the Blackthorns story! LET THEM GOOOO. Also, the epilogue totally sets up The Wicked Powers as City of Lost Souls 2.0 and i am ... not keen. <br /><br />And like I said the last 100 pages were just .. messy. I'm annoyed because I SHOULD have given this a five star .. it was going so well. Everything I came for was there. The angst was top notch, the character interactions were great, and the book was fast paced and exciting. But those last 100 pages were too much and just so cliche and weird. And the ending was complete fanservice, which usually I don't mind, but this was WAY too much. I've said this soo many times but I HATE when books with dramatic "this is going to change everything this is the end of the world" plots have literally no consequences. Like the tagline of this book was literally "everything changes" but in the end nothing happened and everyone got to be happy. LOOK I LOVE PAIN AND SUFFERING OKAY. But I just think it's a super let down and doesn't deliver on my expectations of something Big happening.<br /><br />Okay, I admit the loss of Idris was big and will probably play a big role in the next book .. but again it's the same problem I have with other plot lines. Nothing was finished off in this series ! It was all left for the next one. Which is lazy and unsatisfying. I get her series run on to eachother, but the ending of each individual series should still be satisfying and contained to that series in my opinion. <br /><br /><br /><i>
  <blockquote>“If aught but death part thee and me, Emma,” he said, and pressed his lips to the strands. Emma closed her eyes as she whispered, “Julian. Julian. If aught but death part thee and me.” <br /><br /></blockquote>
</i><br /><br />Alright .. that is IT! This is an extremely gushy and messy review I recognise and own it. You'll just have to live with it. PLEASE chime off in the comments I still need to discuss this book I am still in shock</span>
  <a data-text-id="13906136269146384204" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1875680387" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1875680387" />
    <a title="Beth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/44125660-beth"><img alt="Beth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1600268807p2/44125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1875680387?book_show_action=true">May 29, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Beth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Beth" href="/user/show/44125660-beth">Beth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=2018-reads">2018-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=book-series">book-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=characters-i-loved">characters-i-loved</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=my-heart-hurts">my-heart-hurts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=swoony-swoony">swoony-swoony</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=faves">faves</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/44125660-beth?shelf=the-tears-are-real">the-tears-are-real</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1875680387" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6836479116385028254">I’m sorry… but did you expect anything less that <b>5 Stars</b> for my absolute Queen?!<br/><br/><i>Perhaps being parabatai was a weakness that could trap you. But so was any kind of love, and if love was weakness, it was strength, too.</i><br/><br/>Before I get into this review <b>those illustrations were EVERYTHING! They were so beautiful and the detail!</b> It made me so happy!<br/><br/>So I’m not going to lie this review will more than likely be rusty as I haven’t done one for quite a while now so I shall try none the less. Just a pre warnin</span>
  <span id="freeText6836479116385028254" style="display:none">I’m sorry… but did you expect anything less that <b>5 Stars</b> for my absolute Queen?!<br /><br /><i>Perhaps being parabatai was a weakness that could trap you. But so was any kind of love, and if love was weakness, it was strength, too.</i><br /><br />Before I get into this review <b>those illustrations were EVERYTHING! They were so beautiful and the detail!</b> It made me so happy!<br /><br />So I’m not going to lie this review will more than likely be rusty as I haven’t done one for quite a while now so I shall try none the less. Just a pre warning in the things I like and the things I don’t like there will be minor spoilers so you can just stop at that point if you haven’t ready this already.<br /><br />Going to this I was a bag of nerves, I knew that it would be heart wrenching after what happened in Lord of Shadows but the way in which grief is portrayed throughout was just so raw and dealt with in different ways by all of the characters. I didn’t know where the story would take us with the final instalment and I’d be lying if I said this was what I expected, but that kind of makes me enjoy it even more.<br /><br />Luckily I’d read all of the tales from Ghosts of the Shadow Market which were very useful going into this because of how much background we got in relation to a specific character so knowing what I did I was very very worried in regards to that, it was very interesting seeing it all come together though!<br /><br />What I love so much about this series is the characters, there’s honestly no one (other than Zara and the Cohort) that I dislike, I love stories that have strong relationships and this has so much love between the characters you can’t help but become invested in them.<br /><br />The way in which it ended, I am so surprised, it’s not what I expected what so ever and now I’m super intrigued to find out what’s to come, if there’s not another series I WILL RIOT!<br /><br /><i>“Some lights were never meant to burn for long.”</i><br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br />To start with <b>Emma and Julian</b>, honestly all the way throughout I was so worried for what was to come, their love for one another is just so strong and I just wanted them to be happy, IS THAT TOO MUCH TO ASK! Emma is still the strong character from the previous books, and her development from Lady Midnight to this was amazing particularly in one chapter where she realises something and that she has t overcome that and move away from it. My heart for Julian broke, he goes through such a rough patch and seeing what he does to himself DESTROYED me. His care for his siblings and Emma is just undeniable.<br /><br />Then we have the trio that is of course <i>Cristina, Mark and Kieran</i>! I never in my life thought I would enjoy a trio again from Will, Jem and Tessa, but here we are! The balance between them all is just so pure and perfect. They all just fit together in ways that just balance each other out, Cristina is such a loving character and probable;y the purest soul in this book, she is so open and honest and her love for people, ahhh she’s so lovely! Mark is Mark, the things he does and says, they are just so lovable and you know he just tries his hardest to help, the small gestures he does throughout I was NOT coping! Then finally Kieran, I can honestly say that in this, Kieran is my favourite character, He was just so funny and he really came into his own, his love is fierce and when he feels something strongly he will try his best. There is so much I want to say and rave on about but I’m trying to keep this section spoiler free, but I <u>love him!</u><br /><br /><b>Kit and Ty</b> were the two characters I worried about the most after everything that happened in Lord of Shadows, and I don’t think I’m alone in this thought, Ty has to come to terms with a lot, and boy does it get deep! My heart is broken for him, and it was so sad to see the lengths he went to throughout. Then we have Kit another personal favourite of mine, I am very very intrigued by him. Once again I felt sorry for him, he was trying to help Ty, but at the same time trying to deal with other things going on with himself, he is just too precious!<br /><br />I don’t think I really knew much about <i>Dru, Helen and Aline</i>, just the snippets every now and again. Drug for me was SUCH a good character, I liked her friendships with Ty and Kit and her realising her own self worth, it was just nice to see her being able to do small things to help the people she loves and cared about. Aline was so <b>fierce</b> anything relating to making Helen upset Aline took zero bull shit and I LIVED for it, coming into that environment she handled it so well and I just adored her love for Helen, it was just so sweet. I honestly felt for Helen, she’d been away from her family for such a long period of time and to see her bond with her family made me so happy! At times I felt frustrated for her but the way she handled things I felt so proud!<br /><br />My least favourites… <b>Zara and The Cohort</b> I legit hate them all. They were devious and sneaky (but I love to hate characters) and you can’t not hate them. Now as much as I dislike them some of the things they did were clever but still not a fan, I just want to slap them all and I like to think of myself as quite a nice person aha!<br /><br />Finally <i>Diana, Gwyn, Alec, Magnus, Jace and Clary</i>, I know this is a weird bunch to put together but it’s probably easier this way because it’s just little things. Diana was of course great and what she did YES GIRL! Gwyn once again enjoyed! It was nice to see Jace and Clary again, they’re not my favourite characters but it was still good! Alec and Magnus! I’d forgot how much they were in Lord of Shadows but I honestly love their defiance and how they work together the simple things make me happy! <br /><br />Pre Warning there will be <u>spoilers ahead</u><br /><br /><i>I love you. I love you. I love you.</i><br /><br />What I <b>liked?</b><br />- Some nice little references to previous books (Will Herondale of course)<br />- Ty tryin to get to Livvy, my god my poor little heart, but it was such a Ty thing to do and just ARGH<br />- Seeing the family Dynamics, it was so lovely to see Helen and Aline back<br />- Ty gave Kit his first Witchlight! Come onnnnnnnn<br />- I didn’t mention this earlier BUT the Trio relationship, I never knew I needed this but turns out I 1000000% do, I am here for it! I could go on and on, but I loved Kierans description of why they were perfect as a unit and it was everything!<br />- All of the tension, nothing going right, just forever hoping for some Peace!<br />- Perfect Diego helping Kieran along with Divya, I liked seeing a bit inside the Scholomance<br />- All of the feeeeeeels<br />- Kieran pretending to be asleep because he felt awkward… dead :’)<br />- Helen sitting on Kieran and him asking her to move because it’s painful (these one liners have me every time)<br />- Emma taking the Tapestry… absolute gold!<br />- The names of the Downworlders <i>”My name is Greg. Greg Anderson.” “It’s Elton John, said Aline grabbing a stamp”</i><br /> - Another Kieran moment… calling his brother a Turnip<br />- Goodbye Arm, you know when you know!<br />- Dru and Kieran with the mugs<br />- That LETTER! I was like no no no no no<br />- Seeing the relationships with so many Parabatai is was very interesting and also heart wrenching at the same time!<br />- Now Julian steps up <b>a lot</b> but what he does in this with sending of the letters and the resistance it was so engaging to read, you could see his thought process and you could see just how smart he actually is. Not only that but the BANNER, I was ugly crying, full blown tears!<br />- Dru asking Kit to teach her things and becoming a True Con Woman!<br />- Kit and just how loving and protective he is towards Ty, he knows how to deal with him and just AHHH I CAN’T!<br />- That T-SHIRT! hahahahahahahahahahaha<br />- The cake :’)<br />- Magnus being able to talk to Ty, it was just such a lovely moment because he just seemed to understand, I know a lot of the other characters too, but Magnus is different in his own way and helped Ty a lot.<br />- Kitten calendars!<br /><br />What I <b>didn’t like?</b><br />- I wasn’t particularly fond of Thule, I get why it had to happen and I don’t know if it’s because of how I was feeling at the time, I think because it was mainly focusing on Julian and Emma and I missed the other characters at that time.<br />- KIT DESERVED MORE! I am low key sad at how he parted with the Blackthorns and in particular Ty, but I kind of get it if there’s more books to come because SURELY it will be about them reconnecting maybe? Although I do like that he’s with Jem and Tessa!<br />- My expectations going in… I kind of also thought there’d be more of Annabel and Ash. I’d guessed in Lord of Shadows that Ash was going to be important but we didn’t really see either of them that much.<br />- I also kind of expected more with Manuel, when we see small snippets from his point of view I thought something more was going to happen unless this is setting him up for the next books<br /><br /><i>“The sky was a road and the stars made pathways; the moon was a watchtower, a lighthouse that led you home.” </i><br /><br />Overall I’m so happy with the way this turned out, it was my most anticipated release for the year and it didn’t disappoint! It’s bittersweet that it’s over but hopefully there will be more to come. I need answers, and you can’t leave some of the characters like this!<br /><br /><i>A-T-L-A-S-T</i><br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1530858270?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a> - 5 Stars<br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1736956729?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Shadows</a> - 5 Stars<br />Queen of Air and Darkness - 5 Stars<br />-------<br />Pre Ramble thoughts...<br /><br />WE HAVE TO WAIT TWO YEARS FOR THIS!<br />AFTER THAT ENDING?!<br />---------<br />25.06.2017<br /><b>Helen and Aline snippets on Tumblr, already not coping.</b><br />---------<br />12.11.2017<br />WE HAVE A COVER... it’s so beautiful! Want. Need. THE RED, I CAN'T <b>LIVINGGGGGGGG</b><br />———-<br />12.02.2018<br />TY and KIT snippets... LIVINGGGGGG ❤️<br />—————<br />28.06.2018<br />When you pray to the gods that you've ordered the right Limited edition... if not well I'll be on the hunt!<br />P.S - 6 months (ish) to go!<br />--------<br />20.10.2018<br />After The Land I lost, I need this now. Why may you ask? THEY HAVE DROPPED A HUGE HINT ABOUT SOMETHING AND I AM DYING INSIDE<br />---------</span>
  <a data-text-id="6836479116385028254" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/65321843-a"><img alt="✨ A ✨ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1604503440p2/65321843.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1930668787?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✨ A ✨ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✨ A ✨ " href="/user/show/65321843-a">✨ A ✨ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=gifted">gifted</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=2018-release">2018-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=five-stars">five-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=explicit-ya">explicit-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=three-stars">three-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=tears">tears</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/65321843-a?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1930668787" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17789941174954817367">I actually thought this series had the potential to become one of my favourites, maybe even be as great as TID (lol what was I thinking). Alas, it seems QoAaD follows in the many footsteps of final books of a trilogy - good but not as good as the first two. <br/><br/>⚠<b>
  <u>If you have not read book 1 & 2 (<i>Lady Midnight</i> and <i>Lord of Shadows</i>), do not go any further</u>
</b>⚠<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“This is the nature of having a soul, Kieran, and a heart. We all stumble around in the dark and we cause each other pain and we try to make up</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17789941174954817367" style="display:none">I actually thought this series had the potential to become one of my favourites, maybe even be as great as TID (lol what was I thinking). Alas, it seems QoAaD follows in the many footsteps of final books of a trilogy - good but not as good as the first two. <br /><br />⚠<b>
  <u>If you have not read book 1 &amp; 2 (<i>Lady Midnight</i> and <i>Lord of Shadows</i>), do not go any further</u>
</b>⚠<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>“This is the nature of having a soul, Kieran, and a heart. We all stumble around in the dark and we cause each other pain and we try to make up for it the best we can. We are all confused.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />Chapter one opened up exactly where <i>Lord of Shadows</i> left off. And for some reason I was not expecting that. <br /><br />There I am, reading the first page and I'm already crying? Cruel Cassie, just cruel. <br /><br />I was an emotional wreck during the first few chapters. And had to pause every so often because of how much I was crying. <br /><br /><br />After the chaos that Annabel leaves in her wake, the Blackthorns and Emma are (understandably) grief stricken. But there are still many problems and enemies around. Julian and Emma are sent to Faerie to retrieve the Black volume from Annabel, while the rest of the family and Cristina head back to Los Angeles to find an antidote to the blight and warlock disease. <br /><br />Zara Dearborn and the Cohort become more than just a little problem. They manage to use the chaos to their advantage and the Shadowhunters are now facing a civil war. <br /><br />Just when Emma and Julian are close to a solution to their love predicament, Livvy's death and Annabel's crimes knock everything they had planned off course. And though Emma is also shattered, she has to be strong for Julian and the Blackthorns. <br /><br /><br />I could feel Julian's grief as if it were my own. The lengths he goes to in this book to keep himself together so that he can do what needs to be done was heartbreaking. Honestly Julian is such a great and complex character. I think Cassie really did a good job with his arc. <br /><br /><blockquote>His whole life had been built around exerting control over himself, over the mask he showed the world, and now it was cracking.</blockquote><br /><br />The whole Blackthorn family (+Kit+Diana+kieran) are precious to me. But I'm not going to speak about them in this review. I'm going to just get to <b>the reason why I lowered my rating</b>. <br /><br />The first half of this book was great and I really liked it. But then the excessive cameos and over used themes started to get to me. <br /><br />But the real reason was the most anticipated parabatai curse reveal. After all that build up .... I burst out laughing <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when it turns out they turn into giant nephelim. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. That whole scene was ridiculous I couldn't believe it. It was stupid and weird and ruined the book for me. <br /><br />I get that Cassie will be continuing the Shadowhunters franchise but I'm a little tired of her ending a series with cliffhangers that ensure that people are desperate to read her next books which we have to wait a billion years for. <br /><br />A well rounded off Cassie Clare series is all I ask for, honestly. <br />______<br /><b>My reviews for:</b><br /><br /><i>The Infernal Devices Series</i><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182520676" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Angel</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182522112" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Prince</a><br />Book 3: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3182523415" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a><br /><br /><br /><i>[Sorry no reviews for TMI, I read it too long ago and don't plan to re-read]</i><br /><br /><i>The Dark Artifices Series</i><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2324804598" rel="nofollow noopener">Lady Midnight</a><br />Book 2: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1930668614" rel="nofollow noopener">Lord of Shadows</a><br /><br /><br /><i>The Last Hours Series</i><br />Book 1: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2030617844" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="17789941174954817367" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
