  <span id="freeText3785329514151782617" style="display:none">usually final books in series don't have cliffhangers, but go off cassie, i guess.<br /><br />i'm actually pleased that i like this as much as i did because i was expecting the size would make it really boring and i would end up skipping chapters, but the way this was written actually made every POV integral to the plot so it kept my attention he entire time, except when the resolution happened on page 750 but the book kept on going for 200 more pages. <br /><br />i love that the TMI and TID characters have a lot of gravity in this series. In the moments that i wasn't totally hooked on the blackthorns' plot, magnus or jem or jace would show up and it would immediately electrocute me into caring once again, so I like that they were there a lot. Also, the whole *ahem* middle part of this book was TOTALLY unexpected but genius but also it's gonna haunt me until 2022 when the next book comes out, so thanks. <br /><br />(he really said "i prefer red heads" iM V OM ITING)</span>

<div id="review_2220911854" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2220911854" />
    <a title="Ana" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1991298-ana"><img alt="Ana" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528559847p2/1991298.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2220911854?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ana" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ana" href="/user/show/1991298-ana">Ana</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781471116704" href="/book/show/30214330-queen-of-air-and-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=2018-booklist">2018-booklist</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=fantastique">fantastique</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=read-in-2018">read-in-2018</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=own-and-read">own-and-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1991298-ana?shelf=lgbtqia">lgbtqia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2220911854" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9881601856927116465">More like <b>
  <i>1.5 stars</i>
</b>!?! Believe me, no one is more surprised (and saddened) by this than I am. <b>This might as well be my most disappointing book of 2018.</b> I had to put it down halfway through and finished two other novels. That much I dreaded picking this one back up.<br/><br/>Is it wrong to say that it didn’t feel like a Cassandra Clare TDA book? Compared to LoS, which is still my favourite in this series, this read like a much-diluted version of her TDA Shadowhunter universe, the characters were boring</span>
  <span id="freeText9881601856927116465" style="display:none">More like <b>
  <i>1.5 stars</i>
</b>!?! Believe me, no one is more surprised (and saddened) by this than I am. <b>This might as well be my most disappointing book of 2018.</b> I had to put it down halfway through and finished two other novels. That much I dreaded picking this one back up.<br /><br />Is it wrong to say that it didn’t feel like a Cassandra Clare TDA book? Compared to LoS, which is still my favourite in this series, this read like a much-diluted version of her TDA Shadowhunter universe, the characters were boring me to death with their endless conversations and the plot pacing was all over the place. <b>I couldn’t bring myself to care about any of it.</b> <br /><br />Having this many shifting POVs and subplots (Emma, Julian, Cristina, Mark, Kieran, Kit, Dru, Diana, Helen, Diego, Manuel - completely unnecessary and not very convincing as a rather cowardly psychopath, <b>I am surprised Church didn’t get a say in this</b>) makes for a dull and highly predictable read, because, if not handled properly, it simply repeats things over and over again.<br /><br />I’ll give you an example: take Kieran, Cristina &amp; Mark and make “last night” happen; have Cristina and Mark talk about said last night; have Mark and Kieran talk about it; have Kieran, Cristina <i>and</i> Mark talk about it; have Emma <i>AND</i> Cristina talk about it; have Kieran and Adaon talk, in a roundabout way, about it; have Kieran, Cristina and Mark talk about it some more. See where I’m going with this? There’s so much Kierarktina??? talk in this book that, to me, it overshadows the other relationships and friendships. I get that Cassie wanted to do it right, but it’s just too much. It reads like a fanfic wet dream.<br /><br /><b>The entire Thule episode was ridiculously weird, recycling plot and restoring characters that should have been left where they belonged: in the fictional bin!</b> Also, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[am I the only one who thought of the alternate dimension they pulled off in the TV show while reading this? Granted, here everything a lot darker, less sparkly. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />There were some many emotional moments in LM and LoS that had me basically yell “How dare you?” at my own books. The grief and other intense emotions here were watered down by the constant shifting of perspective: you couldn’t spend enough time in a character’s mind to get a sense of what they’re really feeling. <br /><br />This review could be waaay longer, as I took notes (with loads of exclamation marks &amp; WTFs), but right now I can’t be bothered... I might sound like a broken record with this one, but it needn’t have been a 900+ book! <br /><br />Who’s surprised by the Epilogue? <b>Not me…</b> Ughhh. I was over Clace like four books ago.<br /><br />I feel like we went back to TMI with this one!</span>
  <a data-text-id="9881601856927116465" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1583649783" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1583649783" />
    <a title="ambsreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads"><img alt="ambsreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508924675p2/30813900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1583649783?book_show_action=true">May 23, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1583649783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17662877938198067289"><b>SPOILER REVIEW</b><br/><br/>Trigger Warnings: grief, self mutilation, death, war, murder<br/><br/><a href='http://ambsreads.wordpress.com/2018/12/09/queen-of-air-and-darkness-by-cassandra-clare-spoiler-review/' rel='nofollow noopener'>My review for Queen of Air and Darkness by Cassandra Clare was first posted on my blog. Find it here.</a><br/><br/><br/>Queen of Air and Darkness is the book I have been waiting for all year. I don’t think I have ever anticipated a Cassandra Clare book as much as this one. The ending of Lord of Shadows scared me to my core and if you ask me about it today you have a 110% chance of me bursting into tears at the mere mention of it. This finale</span>
  <span id="freeText17662877938198067289" style="display:none"><b>SPOILER REVIEW</b><br /><br />Trigger Warnings: grief, self mutilation, death, war, murder<br /><br /><a href="http://ambsreads.wordpress.com/2018/12/09/queen-of-air-and-darkness-by-cassandra-clare-spoiler-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">My review for Queen of Air and Darkness by Cassandra Clare was first posted on my blog. Find it here.</a><br /><br /><br />Queen of Air and Darkness is the book I have been waiting for all year. I don’t think I have ever anticipated a Cassandra Clare book as much as this one. The ending of Lord of Shadows scared me to my core and if you ask me about it today you have a 110% chance of me bursting into tears at the mere mention of it. This finale to The Dark Artifices series did not disappoint. It left me reeling and having so many damn questions. You can bet I screamed WHAT at my book around about 100 times a page. I was absolutely shattered.<br /><br />This finale will probably be Cassie’s best. They continue to get better the more she writes and I am so damn happy to be able to experience this journey with everyone as we dive into the Shadowhunter realms. I am also self-proclaimed Shadowhunter trash – while also seeing everything wrong with the books and Cassie, I’m not blinded, don’t worry.<br /><br />As a warning, this review will contain spoilers. The spoilers will be for the previous books in this series so you have been warned. I can’t talk about this book without mentioning certain events. If you haven’t read this series, come back after you do so we can discuss. If you haven’t read this series and don’t want to, read forward and be spoiled, my friends.<br /><br />Queen of Air and Darkness picks up exactly where Lord of Shadows dropped off. With Julian holding Livvy after she has been murdered. We get to experience every ounce of grief that the Blackthorn family feels throughout the book and it is honestly enough to knock you off your feet. I promise you that you will burst into tears several times at work…not that I did that. The finale of The Dark Artifices takes you on a journey. There are countless storylines and at times it is a tad difficult to keep up. Obviously, it is better to have read all the Shadowhunter Chronicles to understand how people relate to certain things but it really isn’t needed. You can jump into this series and scream – obviously don’t just jump into Queen of Air and Darkness without having read the previous books.<br /><br />Throughout this book we get to follow Julian and Emma’s struggle to tamper down their feelings, Ty dealing with his grief for Livvy in the wrong way, Kit being a Herondale, Drusilla coming in to herself, Diana and Gwyn’s love story continue, Cristina, Kieran and Mark drama, Cohort business (seriously this was some Donald Trump shit), some Faerie Drama and finally find out who the mysterious Ash is (we all knew). Within 800 pages a lot has to happen and it does. We get to see all the old characters whom we loved and I even found myself liking Clary and Jace – something I thought was impossible when I read The Mortal Instruments. I can barely even begin to talk about each plot line because there is just so much going on. You will be thrown in a whirlwind and be actively engaged no matter who’s the storyline you are reading. There are plenty of changes throughout the long ass chapters Cassie writes to get a feel for everyone.<br /><br />I should probably start off with the one thing I disliked about Queen of Air and Darkness. I don’t know if I ever publicly spoke about it on my blog but anti-hero Julian was all that I ever wanted in this series. To see Cassie jump outside her comfort zone and write him would fuel me. While we did get somewhat of an antihero Julian it was not what I had imagined. In fact, it was slightly disappointing and something I’m not sure added to the plot. Julian turning off his feelings simply felt weak. You’re telling me the boy who walked miles to get groceries for his siblings would turn off his feelings for them? Try again.<br /><br />That’s all I didn’t like though, so Cassie really did smash it out of the park.<br /><br />Throughout the series, we have had glimpses of Aline and Helen. We have never really gotten to see them which is disheartening as the only f/f couple in the series. We finally get to really meet them and I must say that I adore them. Aline was so damn relatable to me and Helen was just an angel who wanted to care for her siblings, even if they didn’t want her to. The couple themselves were so damn sweet and I adored every moment of their relationship on the page. They were truly so special to read. I am sure we’ll see more of them in future books as well which has me squealing with excitement.<br /><br />There wasn’t much Jem and Tessa in this book either which was fantastic. If you know me, you’d know I hate that ship. I get it. Everyone thinks it is the best love triangle to ever exist in the sense that you can’t ‘choose’. Bitch, I chose and now I can’t like Jem. I hate him. So, having not much of them throughout this book was fantastic. Though I could have done with more Simon and Isabelle, oh well.<br /><br />Interdimensional travel is typically something that turns me off a book. However, Thule was magnificent. A world completely opposite from the one our character lives in where Sebastian Morgenstern won the war. It was chilling. The fact that Cassie thought of that? Ugh, her mind. She is a genius. However, she really didn’t include as much Annabel as I thought she would considering she is on the cover. I wonder where that will come in to play?<br /><br />The relationships in this book as well. Cassie diving in to a poly relationship was fantastic, Cassie’s further development of Emma and Julian was brilliant, Magnus and Alec’s already established relationship filled me with joy and I don’t even like them, and lastly, Drusilla’s future love life will probably be complicated but y’all know I love her.<br /><br />Cassandra Clare carefully crafted it so every single plotline that ran through this story intersected at the end. They all came together in a big way that you know leads off into the next series. I can truly not wait to read whatever she puts out next. I honestly need it in my hands like yesterday. The ending of this particular story left me breathless. I can’t wait to see what hints that we found throughout this book to come to fruition in future books.<br /><br />I would desperately love for Cassie to give us a nice happy ending for the Blackthorns but with the fact that The Wicked Powers is based around Kit and Ty (who I can’t even begin to talk about in this book) tells me this family hasn’t had the last of its dramas.<br /><br />Overall, Queen of Air and Darkness will probably be my favourite book of 2018. I am still reeling from the events and want to scream about them from the rooftops. Heck, this is the first review I’ve sat down to write straight after finishing the book. Cassandra Clare gives us a bit of everything in this finale and even more. I can’t wait to hear everyone’s thoughts and theories on what will happen next.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17662877938198067289" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">

<span id="freeTextContainer10436992029662212905"><blockquote>
<i><b>“Without sorrow, there can be no joy."</b> </i> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1541155160ra/26536638.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/><blockquote>
<i><b>“Shadowhunters are slow to love,” she said, “but once we love, we love forever.”</b> </i> <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462667978ra/19028355.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote><br/><br/>Finally, happily ever after!! <br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>Julian & Emma</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><b><i>“I’m not the same person. I can’t say I feel things I don’t understand.”<br/>“Well, I want the same person,” she said. “I want Julian Blackthorn. My Julian Blackthorn.” <br/> “So who am I to you, then?” he asked, dropping his hand. <br/>“You are the person I have to protect until my Julian comes back to live inside you again,” she s</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText10436992029662212905" style="display:none"><blockquote>
<i><b>“Without sorrow, there can be no joy."</b> </i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1541155160ra/26536638.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
<i><b>“Shadowhunters are slow to love,” she said, “but once we love, we love forever.”</b> </i> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1462667978ra/19028355.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Finally, happily ever after!! <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>Julian &amp; Emma</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><b><i>“I’m not the same person. I can’t say I feel things I don’t understand.”<br>“Well, I want the same person,” she said. “I want Julian Blackthorn. My Julian Blackthorn.” <br> “So who am I to you, then?” he asked, dropping his hand. <br>“You are the person I have to protect until my Julian comes back to live inside you again,” she said. “I don’t want this. I want the Julian I love. You might be in the cage, Jules, but as long as you are like this, I am in the cage with you .” </i> </b> <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1444012540ra/16441331.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
<b><u>Mark &amp; Christina &amp; Kieran</u></b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545158336ra/26768236.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
<b><u>Alec's &amp; Magnus's Wedding &lt;3</u></b> <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466697438ra/19509657.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><i><b>“When one day people look back on me and what my life meant, I don’t want them to say, ‘Alec Lightwood fought in the Dark War’ or even ‘Alec Lightwood was Consul once.’ I want them to think, ‘Alec Lightwood loved one man so much he changed the world for him.’ ”</b> </i> <br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1442585010ra/16255465.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br>Until I read this epilogue!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1545158336ra/26768235.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <u>Ty &amp; Kit (I love them)</u>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><i>
  <b>“I can’t live without Livvy.” <br>“Yes, you can,” Kit whispered. “You can. You think this will make your family stronger, but it will destroy them if you bring her back. You think you can’t survive without Livvy, but you can. We will go through it together.” Kit’s face was cold; he realized he was crying. “I love you, Ty. I love you.”</b>

<div id="review_2030991043" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2030991043" />
    <a title="C.G. Drews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews"><img alt="C.G. Drews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1521552918p2/11375137.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2030991043?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="C.G. Drews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="C.G. Drews" href="/user/show/11375137-c-g-drews">C.G. Drews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=best-of-2019">best-of-2019</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=5-star">5-star</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11375137-c-g-drews?shelf=read-2019">read-2019</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2030991043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1444366891887720592"><b>My opinion on this is basically ONE LONG EXTENDED SCREEEEEAM.</b> Ok I love this series. I absolutely am obsessed with it. My hEarT. Of course finales come with so many expectations, but this was <i>amazing</i>. But then I am Shadowhunter trash and these books can do no wrong afjdskald. I will say that is is <i>incredibly hard to write a review</i>...my brain is a smooshed swirl of emotions.<br/><br/>but basically: GOOD JOB BOOK. YOU RIPPED ME IN HALF AND ALSO HEALED MY SOUL. BLESS.<br/><br/><b> ➸ My ships. MY SHIPS.</b><br/>Look I had expectat</span>
  <span id="freeText1444366891887720592" style="display:none"><b>My opinion on this is basically ONE LONG EXTENDED SCREEEEEAM.</b> Ok I love this series. I absolutely am obsessed with it. My hEarT. Of course finales come with so many expectations, but this was <i>amazing</i>. But then I am Shadowhunter trash and these books can do no wrong afjdskald. I will say that is is <i>incredibly hard to write a review</i>...my brain is a smooshed swirl of emotions.<br /><br />but basically: GOOD JOB BOOK. YOU RIPPED ME IN HALF AND ALSO HEALED MY SOUL. BLESS.<br /><br /><b> ➸ My ships. MY SHIPS.</b><br />Look I had expectations and wishes, and they were <i>met</i>. Although, I mean, I had a lot of cool theories that didn't happen -- GOD I WISH I WROTE FANFIC because I have thoughts. But anyway, I love the romance in these. I know we roll our eyes a lot at the whole "It's the end of the world but you're <i>kissing right now???</i>" thing. But also: it makes sense. Like at one point Cristina told Emma she had romance problems and Emma was like, THANK GOD. LET'S TALK ABOUT THAT INSTEAD OF DEATH. So I get that??? I think it's entirely natural that a bunch of teens who are stressed to the point of breaking will find comfort and longing in kissing one (or two idk go for it, childs) another.<br /><br />also fkkkkk I LOVE MY SHIPS.<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Ok here's the thing though: I WANTED Kieran x Cristina x Mark to get together like nothing else. And they DID. POLY REP OMG. But I also wanted them to be forever-together, because apparently I am built of tree sap. <b>I wanted Kieran to marry Cristina and Mark and they all live as faerie kings/queens.</b> Idk don't judge me. I had my heart set on this. Not just like weekend flings in a cottage smh. So it's like 80% of a win storyline. But yeah :/ How are they going to raise their CHILDREN like this. (They have no kids, hush. I'm just saying.)  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><br />➸ <b>How my heart beats for my Blackthorns.</b><br />The family is so STRESSED here omg and devastated and wrecked. I love how they all tore away from each other and realised it wasn't helping. Helen is a sweetheart gift, I'm so glad she's here to be mum/big sister!! Mark continues to be SO PURE and wholesome afjdksald I love him. (He like makes donut sandwiches and he's so pleased with himself arranging the plates.) I love that Julian just SNAPPED because he held up for so long, it was good to see a human side. Dru got way more of a part and I loved it!! THE BLACKTHORNS ARE EVERYTHING.<br /><br />I also just want to say <b>I really really love Kieren.</b> Far too much afjdklsa my faerie, dramatic deadly son. And Cristina !!!! LOVE CRISTINA!! Also Diana. And Kit is precious and his story has only just begun so afjdklsad I cannot wait for his trilogy even though it's going to be forever till it comes AHHHH.<br /><br /><br /><br />➸ <b> Was it too long???</b><br />Here's the thing: 50% of me loved every. frikkin'. page. Because I want maximum time with my children. However, the book was genuinely uncomfortable to hold. It took me forever to finish it because my brain was screaming "READ MORE!!" but it physically hurt to hold. I knoooow. There are kindles. But I just think it should've been a bit shorter. Or two books? Two books would've been fine.<br /><br /><br />➸ <b>The plot was INTENSE THOUGH.</b><br />So much happened like afjdksald I'm a whirlwind. It's impossible to talk about the details without spoilers though, so I'm just living it as: it was so long, but yet never dull. I loved how it balances the soft moments (with coffee and cuddles and coloured pencil smudges and beach kisses) with the hardcore action moments (fighting in Faerie, slashing swords, using impossible magic, badass battles, heartwrenching traumaaaaa).<br /><br /><br /><b> ➸ I also have NO idea how Cassandra Clare keeps this all straight in her head. 0_0</b><br />I'm just...wow. There are so many threads, so many details (like who has which knife and how that's important later) and it just boggles my mind!! The histories all twine together and reference each other and it's just Good™ and clever.<br /><br /><b>➸ And it doesn't spare the emotions.</b><br />I LAUGHED. I CRIED. I WAS A MESS. I was like anxiety laughing all the time??? There's less sassy comebacks in this one because the book is SO DARK. But god, I live for the one-liners. But seriously it ripped me to pieces AND it was satisfying and good.<br /><br /><br /><b>I THINK THE THING TO TAKE AWAY HERE IS THAT I LIKED THIS BOOK.</b> Just a little. Not much obviously. I'm chill. *hACKS UP A LUNG* It gave me what I desperately wanted with my sons' ships. It gave me maximum Blackthorn time. There was mercy AND vengeance. There were plot twists, cunning schemes, and love. It was the kind of emotional wave that you just stand there, fists clenched, and scream for a very long time bECAUSE YOU FEEL TOO MANY THINGS AT ONCE.<br /><br /><br />ugh ok. I need to go cry until <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/30295312.The_Red_Scrolls_of_Magic__The_Eldest_Curses___1_" title="The Red Scrolls of Magic (The Eldest Curses, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">The Red Scrolls of Magic</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17699853.Chain_of_Gold__The_Last_Hours___1_" title="Chain of Gold (The Last Hours, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Chain of Gold</a> are out.<br /><br /><br /><blockquote> "But I thought -- you said we would be done with each other."<br />"I am not done with you," said Kieran. "I could never be done with you, Mark Blackthorn."</blockquote><br /><br /><blockquote>"I am also an excellent cooke," said Mark, putting an acorn onto his s'more. Everyone stared.<br />"He can't help it," said Cristina loyally. "He has lived with the Wild Hunt for so long."<br />"I don't do that," said Kieran, eating a s'more in the correct fashion. "Mark has no excuse."</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="1444366891887720592" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1774280368" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1774280368" />
    <a title="Caitlin" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57334157-caitlin"><img alt="Caitlin" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1507948675p2/57334157.jpg" /></a>

<span id="freeTextContainer8868309012542191123">I really liked this, best of this trilogy in my opinion, but I'm exhausted. It's so long. There were several points where things felt like it was ending but then I'd notice I still had HOURS left of my audiobook.   <span id="freeText8868309012542191123" style="display:none">I really liked this, best of this trilogy in my opinion, but I'm exhausted. It's so long. There were several points where things felt like it was ending but then I'd notice I still had HOURS left of my audiobook. A lot of the conclusion seemed to be setting up more series set in present day, which I'm all for, but I was more looking forward to how TDA will tie in with the upcoming The Last Hours series. But anyway, I did like this. Just feel overwhelmed.<br /><br /><b>Audiobook review:</b> Narrated by James Marsters again. I think he's great, although it's a little weird to hear a man in his 50s reading teenage sex scenes. And Julian sounds much too old. But honestly, he's a talented narrator.<br /><br />tw: Several things to do with war and violence, but some things that stood out were: cutting, discrimination against entire populations, strong political parallels.</span>

<div id="review_2101773153" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2101773153" />
    <a title="ℨαrα " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/57602032-r"><img alt="ℨαrα " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577832613p2/57602032.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2101773153?book_show_action=true">Sep 19, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ℨαrα " class="user" itemprop="url" name="ℨαrα " href="/user/show/57602032-r">ℨαrα </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781442468436" href="/book/show/36538785-queen-of-air-and-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=5-stars">5-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=heart-wrenching">heart-wrenching</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=cried-a-river">cried-a-river</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=couldnt-put-it-down">couldnt-put-it-down</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=lots-of-family">lots-of-family</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/57602032-r?shelf=blood-blood-blood-death">blood-blood-blood-death</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2101773153" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13196698029413970896"><b>
  <u>Things I liked:</u>
</b> <br/>◘ Cassandra Clare’s writing continues to improve immensely and was beautiful.<br/>◘ Lord Byron and Edgar Allan Poe have been two of my favourite poets since high school, and this book was partially inspired by poems from BOTH of them.<br/>◘ It had an abundance of hard-hitting, emotional moments. But they were also balanced out by the funny, light-hearted, happy, tender moments. <br/>◘ EMMA AND THE BLACKTHORNS. They were the highlight as usual. Their immense love for each other hurts me.<br/>◘ Li</span>
  <span id="freeText13196698029413970896" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>Things I liked:</u>
</b> <br />◘ Cassandra Clare’s writing continues to improve immensely and was beautiful.<br />◘ Lord Byron and Edgar Allan Poe have been two of my favourite poets since high school, and this book was partially inspired by poems from BOTH of them.<br />◘ It had an abundance of hard-hitting, emotional moments. But they were also balanced out by the funny, light-hearted, happy, tender moments. <br />◘ EMMA AND THE BLACKTHORNS. They were the highlight as usual. Their immense love for each other hurts me.<br />◘ Little moments such as Mark’s balloon animals for the kids, or <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Aline’s <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> “goddamn delicious” frittata make the series what it is. <br />◘ Julian’s art and artistic analogies give me life.<br />◘ Emma’s no-nonsense attitude. Sure it gets them into trouble sometimes, but I love her for it?<br />◘ I don’t like picking favourites but if I HAD to pick my single favourite character it would be <s>Church</s> Emma. <br />◘ Marks character development since book 1 was fanfreakingtastic. I remember him using faerie prose and putting Tavvy in bags of sugar, but now he’s referring to Shadowhunters as “we” and not “they”. He’s come so far :”)<br />◘ Magnus was a blindingly glittery star. <br />◘ At one point it felt like things were just on repeat, but then something happens that FLIPS EVERYTHING ON ITS HEAD AND I LOVED IT.<br />◘ That damn <u>strip of red cloth</u> hurt me.<br />◘ The message that the <i>Cold Peace</i> was the opposite of peaceful and instead brought war. <br />◘ The disarray within the Council was captured well, and is reflective of political chaos in today’s societies. <br /><i>“People are terrified. And fear isn’t logical,” <br />“...and we seek to control what we fear.”</i><br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[◘ There were two things that took me completely off guard:<br />1. The whole Thule ordeal was my favourite. It was giving me serious <i>Shrek: The Final Chapter</i> And <i>Gemina</i> vibes.<br />2. The Cohort’s stunt at the end, Kit’s reveal and corrupt Jace, which set up <i>Wicked Powers.</i><br />◘ My darling alternate universe Livvy possessed such bravery, such strength 😭<br />◘ How actual photographic evidence couldn’t convince alternate universe Livvy that Emma and her brother were real, but Julian’s drawings could. That genuinely made me tear up. <br />◘ <u>Livvy’s letter to Ty</u> was beautiful, poetic and so very heartbreaking. The <i>“I love you. I love you. I love you.”</i> from Livvy to her twin. A small part of me died and something in that letter just made me sit there and weep like the walking tragedy I am. <br />◘ The fact that they named the resistance Livia’s Watch 😭 and JULIANS BANNER.<br />◘ Julian being scared out of his mind and being driven to turn his emotions off. <br /><i>“What hurts more,” Magnus asked, “the love or the hate?”<br />“I don’t know,” Julian said.”</i> THAT SCENE.<br />◘ All of the Blackthorns are growing up, dispersing in their own directions and moving on with their lives, and I feel like that aspect was captured really well. The change felt scary, and very <i>very</i> bitter-sweet, like it does in real life.<br /><i>“As long as you know home is always waiting for you,” said Julian.”</i><br />◘ Michael Wayland, Robert Lightwood’s parabatai. I wasn’t expecting an appearance, but when he showed up at Robert’s funeral it was a tragic kind of wonderful. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>
  <u>Things I disliked:</u>
</b><br />◘ In <i>Lady Midnight</i> and <i>Lord of Shadows</i>, you’d be able to read them without having read <i>The Mortal Instruments</i> while still being able to get pretty much the full effect. But I feel like this book was more dependent on fully understanding the events of the past: The Battle of the Burren, the formation of the Cold Peace, Valentine’s Circle <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[and Sebastian’s history. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br />◘ Not going to lie, the book made me roll my eyes more than a few times. <br />◘ I HATE, loathe, abhor, detest, despise the Mark-Christina-Kieran triangle thingamajig I’m sorry. <br />◘ This has been the case with all of Cassandra Clare’s books, but not <i>every single</i> character (including <i>all</i> of the side characters) needs to have a dramatic romantic subplot or love interest. If we replaced some of that stuff with more page time for Emma and the Blackthorns, I would’ve been a happy camper.<br />◘ <i>Why</i> do I have to share a name with the Dearborn witch?<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[◘<i> “I talked to Jem at the meeting,” Emma said. “He told me he would never do it, never.”</i> <br />This is a prime example of characters withholding information from each other for the sake of plot convenience.<br />◘ That flipping parabatai curse and the unoriginality of how it was resolved. Two kids with a forbidden romance and heavenly fire burning within them save everybody with their vast power and are looked upon as angels from then on. Sound familiar? Yup, thought so. <br />◘ This is a pivotal moment that the entire trilogy has been leading up to and it fell SO so so flat for me. I was expecting something more epic and explosive with more consequences. <br />◘<i> “We lost good warriors on the battlefield, but your friends are safe.”</i><br />Sigh. Not sigh of relief. Sigh of dismay and incredulity. Cassandra Clare has never liked killing off major characters, but I thought she broke out of that mould with Livvy’s death. But again, <u>everyone</u> survived the battle. It makes it feel like the book lacks stakes, and it’s plain unrealistic. <br />◘ Yes, I know that we see many tragic deaths in Thule, but that felt like a cop out because all of those characters were alive in their actual world. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br /><b>
  <u>More quotes that I liked (there are a <i>lot</i> of them):</u>
</b><br />◘<i> “She told me once there is a clock in the hearts of parents. Most of the time it is silent, but you can hear it ticking when your child is not with you and you do not know where they are...” <br />◘ “Be careful what masks you wear, child,” Nene said, “lest you lose your true face forever.”<br />◘ “It requires mortality to make art. The knowledge of death, of things limited. There is fire inside us, Emma, and as it blazes, it burns us, and the burning causes pain—but without its light, I cannot see to draw.”<br />◘ “...but sometimes you wanted to focus on something trivial to take your mind off the apocalypse.”<br />◘ “Once you dissolve dye in water, you can’t take it back out.”<br />◘ “He’d always called it her Wall of Crazy, but in a lot of ways Emma thought of it as a wall of sanity,”<br />◘ “I can’t tell you it gets easier. But it does get steadier; you learn how to live with the new rocking of the new earth, the way sailors gain sea legs.”<br />◘ “...and I’m worth talking to without pretending I’m something I’m not. And I’m not going to bother with anyone who doesn’t see that.” </i><br />Wise words from miss Drusilla Blackthorn.<br />◘ <i>“It does no one any good to look backward for too long and forget that the future lies ahead.”<br /><br /><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[◘ “Entreat me not to leave thee,” she said, reaching for the doorknob, “but you’ve left me. You’ve left me, Julian.”<br />◘ “But I felt it. I was living in black and white and now the color is back.”<br />◘ “In the club yesterday you talked about the weight on you, crushing you. In our world, your last words were ‘I’ve never felt so light.’  ”<br />◘ “...but I can’t have Cameron die for the safety of a world that I’m willing to run away from.”<br />◘ “You are in the cage.” <br />[…]<br />“I am in the cage with you.”<br />◘ “I thought I’d be able to think more clearly, without feelings. But the opposite is true. I can’t think at all.”<br />◘ “Maybe Arthur had been right. Maybe mercy was better than revenge.” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></i><br /><br /> <b>The majority of the book:</b> Unreserved 5 stars <br /><b>60-or-so pages during the climax:</b> Dismal, heartbreaking 3.5 stars<br /><b>Overall rating:</b> ★★★★☆¾<br /><br />Uhh for anyone still reading this, my condolences. Pretend that I’m handing you a medal.<br /><br />—————————————<br />Somebody hold me while I mourn over this trilogy being over. But also nobody touch me or talk to me or glance in my direction or breathe or blink. <br /><br />—————————————<br />I have to say that the covers for this series are THE BEST so far. <br />Also CAN WE JUST FAST FORWARD TO NEXT YEAR THIS TIME? Please? I need this in my life.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13196698029413970896" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2167415208" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2167415208" />
    <a title="☆ Annie ☆" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/48546428-annie"><img alt="☆ Annie ☆" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598177552p2/48546428.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2167415208?book_show_action=true">Nov 12, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="☆ Annie ☆" class="user" itemprop="url" name="☆ Annie ☆" href="/user/show/48546428-annie">☆ Annie ☆</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781471177088" href="/book/show/40696414-queen-of-air-and-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48546428-annie?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/48546428-annie?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2167415208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9865443201956370564">3.5 / ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br/><br/><u>Note: This review contains SPOILERS and personal opinions. </u><br/><br/>The Queen of Air and Darkness was not at all what I was expecting, in more ways than one.<br/><br/>First things first, I have to be perfectly honest and admit that The Dark Artifices in general never captured my love as The Infernal Devices and The Mortal Instruments did. Still, I've always rejoiced in how close to my favourite characters this series brought me, all the glimpses of their lives I got to see, all the moments I got to</span>
  <span id="freeText9865443201956370564" style="display:none">3.5 / ⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️⭐️<br /><br /><u>Note: This review contains SPOILERS and personal opinions. </u><br /><br />The Queen of Air and Darkness was not at all what I was expecting, in more ways than one.<br /><br />First things first, I have to be perfectly honest and admit that The Dark Artifices in general never captured my love as The Infernal Devices and The Mortal Instruments did. Still, I've always rejoiced in how close to my favourite characters this series brought me, all the glimpses of their lives I got to see, all the moments I got to, once again, share with them. There is so much value in that, and for that I am forever grateful.<br /><br />And, too, Julian and Emma found a special place in my heart, through all their love and hardships and shared moments, all their ups and downs that made me root for them and wish it could all be resolved in a way that would keep them together, as they so deserved. And it's precisely what Cassie did, in a way so magnificently handled that, even if I could, I would not have changed a single thing.<br /><br />Can I mention, too, the gloriousness that Thule was? It evoked so many many feelings and it made my heart ache in the best way possible, the way that makes it clear that you are affected, and there for it all and anything and everything that happens to those characters you love so well, happens to you, too. That was the case for me, at least. That world was fire and ash and I loved every single heartache it gave me and every single moment Julian and Emma spent there.<br /><br />But... <br />Yes, unfortunately, there is a but.<br /><br />First off, for various reasons, this book felt unnecessarily long; moments repeating themselves, feelings being shared in the same way over and over again... it felts as if we were running around in circles and it became quite tiresome, after a point.<br /><br />Similarly exhausting was, in my eyes, Cassie's intent to provoke. Yes, we've seen it before, themes that reach their extremity until they get handled satisfyingly (more often that not) but still. The Mark/Christina/Kieran trio situation was, in my opinion, created out of thin air, without any real emotional background between all three of them (Vs Kieran and Mark who had a long history of unresolved feelings and love) that would lead to the depth of feeling that could create such a situation like the one they found themselves in. And again, how their decisions to remain together or not kept resurfacing gave me the sense that it kept happening not as an organic result of their uncertainty, but due to a greater intent for us to remain glued and invested in something quite frail, to begin with.<br /><br />I guess the most disappointing part of it all was the wasted potential that this series had, potential that could have taken Cassie's writing into a darker, more mature level, which did not end up happening, after all.<br />The writing in itself read very inconsistently at times, with the characterisation being quite off and leaving me to think that the characters' voices were interchangeable. With the exception of Julian, Emma, the TMI and TID characters who are well established and like a second nature to both Cassie and us, the new set did not reach a depth that would lend each character their own voice. I would have <i>loved</i> to see more of Dru and Kit, who became a support-character and didn't get as much time as I would have liked.<br /><br />It should be noted that this is the impression I got from QoAaD alone. I think Lady Midnight and Lord of Shadows were much more consistent and true to what they set out to do.<br /><br />Having said all that, and with the new openings we saw for many of those characters (Emma and Julian / Ty / Kit / Jace and Clary) I can't WAIT for any and all new series that Cassie has to write.<br />And believe me when I say, if she only wrote Shadowhunter stories for the rest of my days, that would bring me nothing but utter joy.<br /><br />So, for now, I will leave all those people I love and like to their own adventures, until next time.<br />And if I start my TID reread asap because I just don't want to be parted from this world yet and because what better thing to do whilst waiting for Chain of Gold, well.... can you blame me?</span>
  <a data-text-id="9865443201956370564" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1176042202" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1176042202" />
    <a title="Laura" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8429172-laura"><img alt="Laura" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595453256p2/8429172.jpg" /></a>

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1176042202?book_show_action=true">Dec 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Laura" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Laura" href="/user/show/8429172-laura">Laura</a>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1176042202" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14671452641242702343">Quick thoughts before the review:<br/><br/>I liked it more than the previous books but I still have some mixed feelings about it.<br/>The wedding scene at the end was adorable and I am glad Emma didn't break the bond but the while thing in the other dimension was way too off. I felt like it was cheating because we had already faced Sebastian (even with Emma needing closure) and also I just never could take Annabelle seriously enough to think about her as the real threat. So, that fell flat for me. The Seelie Q</span>
  <span id="freeText14671452641242702343" style="display:none">Quick thoughts before the review:<br /><br />I liked it more than the previous books but I still have some mixed feelings about it.<br />The wedding scene at the end was adorable and I am glad Emma didn't break the bond but the while thing in the other dimension was way too off. I felt like it was cheating because we had already faced Sebastian (even with Emma needing closure) and also I just never could take Annabelle seriously enough to think about her as the real threat. So, that fell flat for me. The Seelie Queen is still the biggest danger and I wonder how long can these books feed off that.<br /><br />But yeah, I kind of liked it but still it was nothing stellar.<br /><br />All the Blackthorns stood out as usual and old beloved characters were there doing stuff I guess.</span>
  <a data-text-id="14671452641242702343" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3502781200" />
    <a title="Lia Carstairs" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/75966379-lia-carstairs"><img alt="Lia Carstairs" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1605829031p2/75966379.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3502781200?book_show_action=true">Aug 21, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lia Carstairs" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lia Carstairs" href="/user/show/75966379-lia-carstairs">Lia Carstairs</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781442468436" href="/book/show/36538785-queen-of-air-and-darkness">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/75966379-lia-carstairs?shelf=all-time-fav">all-time-fav</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3502781200" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer634205141868169387"><pre>
  <b>"Without sorrow, there can be no joy."</b>
</pre> <br/>I can now say that I've reread all of Cassie's main series during quarantine. <br/><b>What an accomplishment.😎😂</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598040439ra/29998247.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Ahhhh but <b>why is it that Cassie's endings to a series always make me cry????😭😫</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598049195ra/29998890.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS AHEAD🛑</u>
</b><br/><br/><b><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_' title='Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Clockwork Princess</a>, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24944889.City_of_Heavenly_Fire__The_Mortal_Instruments___6_' title='City of Heavenly Fire (The Mortal Instruments, #6) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>City of Heavenly Fire</a>, and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13541056.Queen_of_Air_and_Darkness__The_Dark_Artifices___3_' title='Queen of Air and Darkness (The Dark Artifices, #3) by Cassandra Clare' rel='nofollow noopener'>Queen of Air and Darkness</a>.....................</b><br/><br/>They're always so beautifully written and especially with <b>QoAaD's</b> ending—the wedding, specifically Malec's wedding🥺—It was just too sweet🥰😭.<br/><br/><p>
  <b>“And when o</b></p></span>
  <span id="freeText634205141868169387" style="display:none"><pre>
  <b>"Without sorrow, there can be no joy."</b>
</pre> <br>I can now say that I've reread all of Cassie's main series during quarantine. <br><b>What an accomplishment.😎😂</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598040439ra/29998247.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ahhhh but <b>why is it that Cassie's endings to a series always make me cry????😭😫</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598049195ra/29998890.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>
  <u>🛑WARNING: SPOILERS AHEAD🛑</u>
</b><br><br><b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18335634.Clockwork_Princess__The_Infernal_Devices___3_" title="Clockwork Princess (The Infernal Devices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Clockwork Princess</a>, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24944889.City_of_Heavenly_Fire__The_Mortal_Instruments___6_" title="City of Heavenly Fire (The Mortal Instruments, #6) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Heavenly Fire</a>, and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13541056.Queen_of_Air_and_Darkness__The_Dark_Artifices___3_" title="Queen of Air and Darkness (The Dark Artifices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen of Air and Darkness</a>.....................</b><br><br>They're always so beautifully written and especially with <b>QoAaD's</b> ending—the wedding, specifically Malec's wedding🥺—It was just too sweet🥰😭.<br><br><p>
  <b>“And when one day people look back on me and what my life meant, I don’t want them to say, ‘Alec Lightwood fought in the Dark War’ or even ‘Alec Lightwood was Consul once.’ I want them to think, ‘Alec Lightwood loved one man so much he changed the world for him.’ ”</b>
</p><br><br>Cassie is really trying to make me an emotional wreck.🥺😭 <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/24885537.City_of_Bones__The_Mortal_Instruments___1_" title="City of Bones (The Mortal Instruments, #1) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">City of Bones</a> Alec and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13541056.Queen_of_Air_and_Darkness__The_Dark_Artifices___3_" title="Queen of Air and Darkness (The Dark Artifices, #3) by Cassandra Clare" rel="nofollow noopener">Queen of Air and Darkness</a> Alec are such different people.......Cassie just leaves me in awe with the amazing character development.😍 From being a shy and self-conscious teenager, he's now grown up to be the new Consul and an inspiration to many Shadowhunters all over the world. <b>AHHHH I can't🤧🤧🤧</b> I love Alec so much.💕 And of course, <b>Magnus Lightwood-Bane</b> is no different.🥰<br><br><p>
  <b>“Okay, let’s talk about the important part.” Magnus turned to Alec with a furious look on his face. “You killed yourself? Why would you do that?”<br><br>Alec looked startled. “That wasn’t me,” he pointed out. “It’s an alternate universe, Magnus!”<br><br>Magnus grabbed Alec by the front of his shirt. “If I die, you are not allowed to do anything like that! Who would take care of our kids? How could you do that to them?”<br><br>“We never had kids in that world!” Alec protested.</b>
</p>xD and delirious Magnus is hilarious😂:<br><p>
  <b>“The Children of Lilith will indeed be in debt to the Children of the Courts after this day, Kieran Kingson,” said Magnus, staring intently in what he clearly thought was Kieran’s direction.<br><br>“That was a very nice speech, Bane,” said Jace. “Unfortunately, you’re talking to a doughnut.”</b>
</p><br>Then there's seeing the rest of the TMI crew throughout the book. <b>Simon &amp; Izzy</b> and <b>Clary &amp; Jace</b> were the same as always.🤣 Their trick against the Cohort was the best.😂<br><p>
  <b>Manuel made a sputtering noise. “Kill them,” he said, turning to his companions. “Go on. Kill them.”<br><br>Jace drew the third in a line of X’s on the ground and tossed aside his stick. “Checkmate,” he said.<br><br>“Checkmate is chess,” Clary pointed out, entirely ignoring the Cohort surrounding them.<br><br>Jace grinned. It was a bright, beautiful grin, the sort of grin that made Helen understand why, all those years ago, Aline had kissed him just to see. “I wasn’t talking about our game,” he said.<br></b>
</p><br>Argh that reminds me of the <b>stupid Cohort</b>. I was <b>SO HAPPY</b> when <b>Horace Dearborn</b> was killed by Julian (his spine was snapped in half muahahahha😈). <br><br>I was really hoping for Zara and Manuel to die, but unfortunately Emma decides to spare her life......and what does she do? <b>SHE STABS EMMA IN THE BACK. ISTG ZARA U BACKSTABBING (literally) COWARD👿🤬🤬😤</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1598053485ra/29999180.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I swear, she better get the death she deserves in <b>The Wicked Powers</b> or <b>I WILL RAGE</b>. SHE <b>NEEDS</b> THE <b>MOST PAINFUL</b> DEATH POSSIBLE.😤<br><br>But you know, I'm really curious to what their plan is seeing how they're stuck in Alicante.🤔<br><br>OH and I just <b>LOVED</b> ANNABEL'S DEATH. AND IT WAS BY THE HANDS OF JULIAN!!!🔥 <b>LIVVY HAS BEEN AVENGED</b>😭 (Altho Ty had to ruin her peace and bring her back as a ghost😫😢 Poor Livvy.)<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1598054098i/29999257._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love how this art by <i>
  <a href="http://www.alice-duke.com/book-illustration" rel="nofollow noopener">Alice Duke</a>
</i> was the dust jacket for <b>QoAaD. I'm so in looooveeee😍😍😍</b><br><br>Omg and <b>Jemma</b>!!!😍 Julian and Emma have been through so much together dealing with the <i>parabatai</i> curse. I'm so happy everything turned out well and they got the happiness they deserved.🥺🥰<br><pre>
  <b>At the edge of everything, love and faith have always brought me back.</b>
</pre><br>If I had to choose the characters I'm most looking forward to in <b>TWP</b>, it'd definitely be <b>Ash Morgenstern, Dru, and Kit!!!</b> Really curious to see what's gonna happen between those three. Oh, and I wonder how <b>Ty and Ghost Livvy</b> are going to be dealing with their bond. Hmmmmm🤔<br><br>Ahhh but the epilogue seriously just kills me though.😣 Cassie just leaves everything off like that and expects us <b>to wait until 2022 (but like it'll probably be 2023)?!?!</b> The torture😫😭😭<br><br><b>
  <u>One thing is certain:</u>
</b><br><br><b>The Wicked Powers</b> is definitely going to <b>destroy</b> me in a way that I could've never imagined possible. <br><br><b>And I am so <i>not</i> ready.<br><br><br><a href="https://chainofnovels.wordpress.com/2020/08/22/queen-of-air-and-darkness-the-dark-artifices-3-by-cassandra-clare-spoiler-review/" rel="nofollow noopener">| Blog |</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="634205141868169387" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('hH/RAKMOlq2/FplwwvkEiwflfzVx2N7DFlGq4tYVloUtI+5CFYiRp1OG9bx6mLXPbNBKl/ZqxRjt84FOzMZjag==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('RgriEFm4Hl0Tm1p2lfcdK0MNBlJrwkaJ8Wx8RQyRjC/vVt1S7z4ZV/8LNrotlqxvKDgz8OxwXVIKzlfpFkJ5wA==')})
  }

But Lord Westfall carries shadows from his own past, and Yrene soon comes to realize they could engulf them both.\n\nIn this sweeping parallel novel to the New York Times bestselling Empire of Storms, Chaol, Nesryn, and Yrene will have to draw on every scrap of their resilience if they wish to save their friends. But while they become entangled in the political webs of the khaganate, deep in the shadows of mighty mountains where warriors soar on legendary ruks, long-awaited answers slumber. Answers that might offer their world a chance at survival—or doom them all . . .<\/span>\n  <a data-text-id=\"11988364342751556339\" href=\"#\" onclick=\"swapContent(\$(this));; return   <span id="freeText14329835926272186810" style="display:none">Hello Goodreadsers. Here's my official bio:<br /><br />"Cassandra Clare was born overseas and spent her early years traveling around the world with her family and several trunks of fantasy books. Cassandra worked for several years as an entertainment journalist for the Hollywood Reporter before turning her attention to fiction. She is the author of City of Bones, the first book in the Mortal Instruments trilogy and a New York Times bestseller. Cassandra lives with her fiance and their two cats in Massachusetts."<br /><br />You can find me online at <br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.cassandraclare.com">www.cassandraclare.com</a><br /><br />I have a blog:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/">http://cassandraclare.livejournal.com/</a><br /><br />and a Facebook:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare">http://www.facebook.com/Cassandraclare</a><br /><br />and a Twitter:<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.twitter.com/cassieclare">www.twitter.com/cassieclare</a><br /><br />I'll be available here on Goodreads to answer questions for a Goodreads Author Discussion starting September 18 — <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/37113.Q_A_with_Cassandra_Clare">http://www.goodreads.com/group/show/3...</a><br /><br />Go sign up so you don't miss the conversation when it starts!</span>
